# V

[Back to index](index.md)

## va

### Sense 1: lexicon

- **Pronunciation:** `VA`
- **Part of speech:** particle
- **Definition:** intended action
- **Register/status:** grammar; accepted
- **Domains:** daily-life
- **Literal:** grammatical particle: aspect
- **Example:** Na va pat ko ti.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)

### Sense 2: particle

- **Pronunciation:** `VA`
- **Part of speech:** particle:aspect
- **Definition:** intended action
- **Register/status:** aspect; accepted
- **Domains:** daily-life
- **Literal:** Marks intended, planned, or conditional action.
- **Example:** Na va pat ko ti.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)

## vaaalau

### Sense 1: lexicon

- **Pronunciation:** `VAAALAU`
- **Part of speech:** verb
- **Definition:** to value assets, judge worth, or estimate standing under exchange or stewardship
- **Register/status:** plain; accepted
- **Root family:** `VALU`; Economics/provision; valuation, judged worth; valuation, judged worth of asset, work, risk, company, or common good
- **Pattern:** verb
- **Literal:** V-A-L-U root, action vowel a
- **Example:** Na vaaalau.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)

## vaaalau-da

### Sense 1: lexicon

- **Pronunciation:** `VAAALAU-DA`
- **Part of speech:** civic/legal term
- **Definition:** valuation report or appraisal record
- **Register/status:** civic; accepted
- **Root family:** `VALU`; Economics/provision; valuation, judged worth; valuation, judged worth of asset, work, risk, company, or common good
- **Pattern:** civic
- **Literal:** V-A-L-U root, public/legal suffix -da
- **Example:** Pu vaaalau-da.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)

## vaaaran

### Sense 1: lexicon

- **Pronunciation:** `VAAARAN`
- **Part of speech:** verb
- **Definition:** to measure variance, spread values, or account dispersion around a center
- **Register/status:** plain; accepted
- **Domains:** education-training, ai-cognition, philosophy-metaphysics, science-math, travel-place
- **Root family:** `VARN`; Mind; variance, measured spread; variance, spread of values, measured distance from the center
- **Pattern:** verb
- **Literal:** V-A-R-N root, action vowel a
- **Example:** Na vaaaran.
- **Corpus:** active (4 attestations); tracks: civic-law, ritual-vow; examples in civic-1453, ritual-1453

- **Pronunciation:** `VANADAR-LEK`
- **Part of speech:** noun
- **Definition:** doctrine, theory, or explanatory frame of: vendor, governed seller
- **Register/status:** plain; accepted
- **Domains:** law-governance, economics-provision, travel-place
- **Root family:** `VNDR`; Law/civic life; vendor, governed seller; vendor, governed seller, provider of goods or services under public terms
- **Pattern:** doctrine
- **Literal:** V-N-D-R root, doctrine suffix -lek
- **Example:** Vanadar-lek lek e rih.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)
